Thefourteentii day of the dark half of the month of Bhado 
and the next day of conjunction are called '‘DagjaH ki rat ” 
It IS a general belief m the hills that on these Wo days dags, or 
witches, whu know magic, wander by night and devour any 
beautiful thing that comes before their sight To avert this 
danger, the Dmwaii or a Brahman gives the people either 
some lice or some mustard seed, pronouncing the following

Bakkh Ram, rakkh deb, rakkh shish, rakkh Mhesh, rakkh
